# All Codex Tasks 001–260

Use this as a reference file. Prefer the individual task files when feeding Codex.

# Codex Task 001 — DesktopAppShell + Theme Foundation

## Global guardrails

Remember: this is a **Windows/Linux desktop-only community chat app**.

- Do **not** create mobile UI.
- Do **not** create web-first responsive UI.
- Do **not** use Discord branding, logos, copied assets, or exact Discord colors.
- Keep the existing MVP UI with Coolicons stable unless the task explicitly says otherwise.
- Do only this task.
- Do not refactor unrelated working code.
- Do not add unrelated advanced roadmap features.
- After finishing, list changed files and explain how to test.

## Phase

MVP desktop UI and desktop foundation

## Goal

Create the Windows/Linux desktop-only app shell with 4 columns, custom title bar placeholder, light/dark design token foundation, no mobile layout.

## Requirements

- Implement or document only the scope described by this task.
- Preserve existing working MVP flows unless the task is specifically a QA/fix task.
- Keep mock mode working when relevant.
- Keep API mode working when relevant.
- Use typed TypeScript boundaries where code is added.
- Use existing services/stores/components where possible.
- If a dependency, native API, backend service, or production credential is unavailable, add a safe placeholder and document the gap instead of breaking the app.
- If this task is documentation-only, do not change application behavior.

## Acceptance criteria

- The task goal is satisfied or the remaining gap is documented clearly.
- No mobile UI is introduced.
- No Discord branding/assets/exact colors are introduced.
- Existing desktop layout remains stable.
- Build/typecheck issues introduced by this task are fixed or listed as known blockers.
- Changed files and test steps are reported.

## Suggested Codex instruction

```text
Create the Windows/Linux desktop-only app shell with 4 columns, custom title bar placeholder, light/dark design token foundation, no mobile layout.

Work within the existing project structure. Do not delete existing work. If a file conflict appears, explain it before overwriting.
```


---
